Param/Value/3B156E90=Champion
Param/Value/3B2C9FA3=<c val="FF0000">Fainted</c>
Param/Value/3B7E031F=<s val="TechDescription"><c val="00FF00">
Param/Value/3B873FBD=<s val="ModLeftSize20"><c val="FFFFFF">Surviving your first day</c></s><n/>Life is tough in the forest. There are many dangers for an inexperienced kobold.<n/>The first thing you should try to do is to gather some resources. Lumber can be gained by chopping down certain trees, and is used for building structures and crafting equipment. Stone can be mined from stone deposits by right-clicking them. Wool is gained from killing sheep, and leather from various animals such as wolves. These are the basic resources that you'll need to survive. Remember to keep an eye on your stamina, running around gathering resources can be very tiring work (especially mining). Build a tent and rest under it to recover your stamina when it is low. When night falls, it is best to build a campfire. Direwovles roam the forest at night and can easily overwhelm a lone kobold. But they are afraid of fire! Build the campfire near your tent so that you can rest while huddled near the fire during the cold night. Another reason for the campfire is to stay warm, for the nights can be very chilly. Now, as you've been killing sheep and wolves for resources you've probably found some raw meat as well. Take the time during the first night to cook that on the campfire and eat it when you get hungry. This is done by left-clicking the food in your backpack (the backpack can be found at the bottom-right part of the screen, just above the command card).<n/><n/><s val="ModLeftSize20"><c val="FFFFFF">Forest life</c></s><n/>Now that you know the basics of survivial, it is time to start crafting some equipment. You can craft equipment either at a workbench or smithy. At the workbench you make items from resources such as lumber, wool and leather. At the smithy you forge items from resources such as iron, shadowstone and radiant gems. These resources can take some exploring to find. Iron ore and shadowstone can be found by simply mining stone deposits. To find a radiant gem you'll need to discover a gold deposit and mine that! There are also gigantic trees growing around the forest, you'll know them when you see them. They take some time to chop down, but provide you with infused lumber in addition to a lot of normal lumber. Infused lumber has magical properties and can be used to craft more advanced equipment. By now you've probably leveled up a few times and have skill points to spend. It can be a good idea to put a few points in forestry and mining to gather resources more quickly, but it is entirely up to what you feel that you need the most. If you're having trouble finding a resource, you can always buy it at a storage outpost for gold. Alternatively, you can sell resources there too if you have too much of something.<n/><n/><s val="ModLeftSize20"><c val="FFFFFF">A new quest</c></s><n/>After a time, things will start happening in the forest. Individuals from all over the land will come seeking your aid in some matter. They usually offer some kind of reward to whichever tribe completes the task first, so hurry! Sometimes, evil beings of great power will invade the forest, and it is your duty to protect the land from these threats. Some might even carry mysterious and powerful loot that can turn the tide of the battle against the rival tribe. Be wary though, for these evil creatures possess great power. It would be folly to try to defeat them alone.<n/><n/><s val="ModLeftSize20"><c val="FFFFFF">The Ancient Spirits</c></s><n/>Death is not necessarily the end for a kobold. There are ancient and powerful spirits in the forest that can help bring you back to life, at a price. There are shrines in the northren and southern parts of the forest where you can communicate with these spirits and resurrect your fallen tribesmen.<n/><n/><s val="ModLeftSize20"><c val="FFFFFF">Travelling wizards</c></s><n/>All kobolds have the potential to learn spells, but only when taught by a powerful wizard. Attract these wizards by building taverns. Having a lot of gold will also make them more likely to stay at your taverns when night falls.

Param/Value/FD23247A=Update 1.34 - "The Art of Fortress Warfare"<n/><n/>New stuff:<n/>	- New 'Fortress Warfare' game mode. Build a Fortress and defend it while destroying the enemy Fortress.<n/>	  Automatic respawn. K/D statistics are not affected in this mode.<n/>	- Support for up to 12 players.<n/>	- New craftable item/structure: Trebuchet - Excellent for breaking enemy fortifications.<n/>	- Palisades can now be transformed into gates that can be opened and closed.<n/>	- New mini-bosses during the "Night of the Dead" quest. Drops Artisanship 20 gear.<n/>	- New monster type during the "Veil of Darkness" quest. Drops Radiant Gems.<n/>	- New reward: Exotic Murlocs (new murloc slave skin).<n/>	- New reward: Wall Patrol (put candles on your palisade end posts).<n/><n/>New craftable items:<n/>	- Twin Throwing Axes: Smithy, 20 Artisanship. Occupies both Main and Off-hand slots.<n/>	- Ironbark Armor: Workbench, 15 Artisanship.<n/><n/>Item changes:<n/>	- Wolfsbane now also makes wolves not fear enemy campfires, torches or lanterns within a 20 radius.<n/>	- Venomous Arbalest now deals 200% attack damage over 20 seconds and increases the target's eating cooldown by 20%.<n/>	- Iron Banded Buckler now blocks all damage from a normal attack instead of just half.<n/>	- Iron-Studded Vest now completely blocks spells (including Affliction and Clairvoyance), but has a 45 sec cooldown.<n/>	- High Ranger's Chainmail -> Master Ranger's Maille no longer enrages your pets when they are low.<n/>	  Instead it will spawn a new pet of the same type when one of yours dies.<n/>	  It also lets you tame pets with your bare hands and gives different stats depending on what pets you have.<n/>	- Gleaming Spear -> Golden Polearm (new model). Gives +1 gold per sec while near enemies. More armor shred, but doesn't stack.<n/>	- Sharp Iron Pickaxe now also gives a 30% chance not to consume a stack of a mineral deposit when mining.<n/>	  The bleed effect on it now also stacks.<n/>	- Light Leather Shield no longer breaks and snares, but instead reduces an attacker's stamina by 5 every time they hit you.<n/>	- Judgment Gavel now requires artisanship skill 15.<n/>	- Demonward now reduces damage taken from undead as well as demons.<n/>	- Outlandish Heartpiercer no longer gives bonus maximum life to pets and doesn't increase damage dealt from behind.<n/>	  Instead it gives your Siphon Life 5 charges and Shadow Cloak stuns the target for 1.5 seconds.<n/>	- Frost Needle has been remade into a channeled ranged support weapon.<n/>	- Dull Pickaxes and Spell Books no longer drop on death.<n/>	- Celestial Orb has reduced base healing, but increased scaling with spell power.<n/>	- Stormwizard's Robes lightning strikes deal more damage.<n/><n/>Visuals:<n/>	- All structures and most units have received new textures and should look better on higher settings.<n/>	  Also added target volumes to the custom models so that arrows and such spread out across the model.<n/>	- Added teamcolor to the kobold vest.<n/>	- Added a fishing animation to the kobold.<n/>	- Arrow projectiles now leave a small trail behind them.<n/>	- Automated Defense Turret has a new model.<n/>	- Taverns how have lanterns that lights up when there's a wizard there.<n/>	- New wolf model.<n/>	- New food models for more consistency within food types (lamb meals all look exactly the same, wolf meals too, etc).<n/>	  It is now easier to distinguish raw/cooked meat by the glow they have on the ground.<n/>	- Lanterns now shine more brightly at night to indicate their active status.<n/>	- The Bloodthirsty Pirate Hat now has a pair of matching shoulderpads.<n/>	- New model for Judgment Gavel.<n/>	- New model for Vicious Javelin.<n/>	- Kobolds, murlocs, stags and bears have longer death animations.<n/>	- Fixed the starcraft 2 bug causing some text to be cut off and end with "..." using a workaround.<n/>	- The Pack Horse is now a Pack Beaver.<n/><n/>Other changes:<n/>	- The strength of bosses now scales with the average team size of remaining teams, instead of total number of living kobolds.<n/>	- New trees start growing by themselves if there are fewer than 200 in the forest.<n/><n/>Not enough space for all changes. Check the Arcade page or the forums for all changes.
